------------------------------
TIP
------------------------------
Let's talk about reflexive verbs!
Verbs that need reflexive pronouns use être in the past. If the subject is feminine, add an ‑e . If the subject is plural, add an ‑s !

--- Table ---
                          | se lever                 
je                        | me suis lev é(e)         
tu                        | t' es lev é(e)           
il / elle                 | s' est lev é(e)          
nous                      | nous sommes lev é(e)s    
vous                      | vous êtes lev é(e)s      
ils / elles               | se sont lev é(e)s        
-------------

Make requests

--- Example Phrase ---

English:     Could you tell us where the golf course is?
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Voudriez-vous visiter la ville ?
English:     Would you like to visit the city?
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Quel est le prix moyen pour un petit déjeuner dans un café ?
English:     What is the average price for one breakfast in a coffee shop?
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Pouvez-vous m'aider, s'il vous plaît ?
English:     Can you help me, please?
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Pouvons-nous garder nos sacs à dos dans le musée ?
English:     Can we keep our backpacks in the museum?
----------------------

------------------------------
TIP
------------------------------
Prends le nôtre !
We've already seen phrases like le mien and les tiennes. Learn a few more phrases to express which things are whose:

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Leurs meubles sont vieux, les nôtres sont neufs.
English:     Their furniture is old,oursis new.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Notre maison est petite, la vôtre est plus grande.
English:     Our house is small,yoursis bigger.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Nos parents sont âgés, les leurs sont plus jeunes.
English:     Our parents are old,theirsare younger.
----------------------
For these, there's no change based on gender , but there is an ‑s with plural nouns !

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Notre hôtel est moins cher que le vôtre.
English:     Our hotel is less expensive thanyours.
----------------------

Ow, my knee!

Communicate in class

------------------------------
TIP
------------------------------
Ils éteignent la lumière
Verbs that end in ‑eindre , like p eindre and ét eindre , have a different pattern from other ‑re verbs like vendre !

--- Table ---
verb éteindre             | verb vendre              
j'éteins                  | je vends                 
tu éteins                 | tu vends                 
il / elle éteint          | il / elle vend           
nous éteignons            | nous vendons             
vous éteignez             | vous vendez              
ils / elles éteignent     | ils / elles vendent      
avoir éteint              | avoir vendu              
-------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Nous éteignons l'ordinateur.​
English:     We are turning off the computer.​
----------------------

------------------------------
Arrête‑toi !
There's a difference between s' arrêter and arrêter . You use arrêter to stop something or someone, and you use s' arrêter to stop yourself.

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      La voiture s'arrête au feu rouge.
English:     The car stops at the red light.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Ils ont décidé d'arrêter la grève.
English:     They decided to stop the strike.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Je me suis arrêté parce que j'étais trop fatigué.
English:     I stopped because I was too tired.
----------------------

KEY PHRASES
------------------------------
Discuss emergencies

French:      Elle s'est coupée.
English:     She got cut.

English:     If the sound is too loud, your ears will hurt!

TIP
------------------------------
Ouch!
Remember, verbs like se blesser or se couper use être in the passé composé . And they change depending on gender and number !

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Nous nous sommes brûlés.​
English:     We got burned.​
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Elle s'est blessée.
English:     She got hurt.​
----------------------
But if you know exactly which body part was affected, there's no ending changes!

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Ils se sont coupé les cheveux.​
English:     They cut their hair.​
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Elle s'est brûlé la main.
English:     She burned her hand.
----------------------

------------------------------
TIP
------------------------------
I broke my leg!
Some verbs can be used with or without se ! If you use se , the action is done to yourself. If there's no se , the action is done to something else.

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Elle a coupé la viande.
English:     She cut the meat.​
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Elle s'est coupée.
English:     She cutherself.​
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Il s'est cassé les jambes.
English:     He broke his legs.
----------------------

Let's talk about Objects!

Use lui to say to him , for her , etc., and leur to say to/for them .​​

TIP
------------------------------
Let's talk about Future Tense!
Some common verbs have irregular bases when talking about the future, but they all use the same endings.

--- Table ---
subject                   | ​ verb ( voir ) ​        
je                        | verr ai                  
tu                        | verr as                  
il / elle                 | verr a                   
nous                      | verr ons                 
vous                      | verr ez                  
ils / elles               | verr ont                 
-------------
Several common verbs have irregular future bases:

------------------------------
TIP
------------------------------
Let's talk about Relative Pronouns!
Use où in phrases like I know where they are or the day when they arrived .
In English, we say the person who helps me and the person who (or whom ) I help , but in French there are two words for who .
It's the same with ce qui and ce que !

------------------------------
TIP
------------------------------
Let's talk about Commands!
When giving commands like buy it or give it to me , pronouns come after the verb and ​ le / la / les always come before te , nous , lui etc!
With negative commands, like don't give it to me , le / la / les come after me / te / se / nous / vous , but before lui and leur .​​

TIP
------------------------------
Let's talk about Agreement!
In phrases like I bought it or I ate them , if the object is feminine , add an ‑e to the verb . If it's plural , add an ‑s !
You have to do this whenever the object that you're talking about comes before the past tense verb , but not when it comes after the verb .

Explore grammar tips and key phrases for this unit


------------------------------
KEY PHRASES
------------------------------
Use the conditional

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Avec des murs aussi minces, on entendrait tout !
English:     With walls so thin, we would hear everything!
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Moi, j'ouvrirais les fenêtres plus souvent.
English:     Me, I would open the windows more often.

--- Example Phrase ---

English:     If I were you, I would get the white curtains.

--- Example Phrase ---

English:     We would get lost in so big a house.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Eux, ils ne peindraient pas sur les murs de leur chambre.
English:     They would not paint on their bedroom's walls.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Cette lampe éclairerait mieux le fond de la pièce.
English:     This lamp would light up the back of the room better.
----------------------

------------------------------
TIP
------------------------------
Let's talk about the subjunctive!
With phrases expressing doubt, possibilities, or desire, use the subjunctive after que . For many verbs , take the ‑ent off the ils / elles present tense form, and use these endings:

--- Table ---
subject                   | verb ( choisir )         
je                        | choisiss e               
tu                        | choisiss es              
il / elle / on            | choisiss e               
nous                      | choisiss ions            
vous                      | choisiss iez             
ils / elles               | choisiss ent             
-------------
Sometimes the subjunctive form looks exactly like the present.

Let's talk about the conditional!
Use the conditional to express what you’d do in hypothetical situations. The conditional uses the same base as the future, but the endings of the imparfait .

--- Table ---
subject                   | verb ( parler )          
je                        | parler ais               
tu                        | parler ais               
il / elle / on            | parler ait               
nous                      | parler ions              
vous                      | parler iez               
ils / elles               | parler aient             
-------------

KEY PHRASES
------------------------------
Use the subjunctive

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Il faut que tu lui écrives le plus tôt possible.
English:     You must write to him as soon as possible.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Je ne veux pas que mon mari prenne sa retraite.
English:     I don't want my husband to retire.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Normalement, il veut qu'on se réunisse le lundi.
English:     Normally, he wants us to assemble on Mondays.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Je ne pense pas qu'il reçoive ce courrier demain.
English:     I don't think he is receiving this piece of mail tomorrow.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Je doute qu'elle prévoie de postuler à ce poste.
English:     I doubt she plans to apply for this position.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Il est possible que nous fassions grève, Monsieur.
English:     It is possible that we will go on strike, sir.
----------------------

------------------------------
TIP
------------------------------
Let's talk about the past tense!
To say things like she had eaten , use the plus‑que‑parfait! It’s like the passé composé , but avoir or être are in the imparfait form.

English:     She brought up the package.

------------------------------
TIP
------------------------------
Let's talk about the subjunctive!
You need to use the subjunctive verb form after phrases expressing negated opinions.
You also need to use the subjunctive after expressing desire, doubt, or possibility with que .
The expressions pour que , bien que , and nul que use the subjunctive afterwards.

TITLE: Unit 44 Guidebook

Explore grammar tips and key phrases for this unit


------------------------------
KEY PHRASES
------------------------------
Blame others

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Si tu avais écouté, tu aurais déjà compris.
English:     If you had listened, you would have already understood.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Si on le lui avait acheté, il l'aurait déjà cassé.
English:     If we had bought it for him, he would have already broken it.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      S'ils n'avaient pas oublié la clé, ils seraient entrés.
English:     If they hadn't forgotten the key, they would have gone in.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Si vous étiez venus, vous auriez eu des macarons.
English:     If you had come, you would have had some macarons.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Si vous aviez répondu, on aurait su où vous étiez.
English:     If you had responded, we would have known where you were.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      S'il s'était levé tôt, il serait arrivé à l'heure.
English:     If he had gotten up early, he would have arrived on time.
----------------------

------------------------------
TIP
------------------------------
Let's talk about the conditional!
To talk about things you would have done , it's like the passé composé but avoir or être are in the conditional form.

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Si tu avais demandé, j’aurais raconté mon histoire.
English:     If you had asked, I would have told my story.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Si vous aviez voulu, nous aurions acheté des fleurs.
English:     If you had wanted, we would have bought flowers.
----------------------
Verbs of motion or change of state use être instead of avoir in phrases like I would have gone .

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      Si elle avait su, elle serait arrivée plus tôt.
English:     If she had known, she would have arrived earlier.
----------------------

--- Example Phrase ---
French:      S’il avaient appelé, nous serions allés avec lui.
English:     If he had called, she would have gone with him.
----------------------
